***uitzitten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitzitten.html>uitzitten</a> (12881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitzitten.html>uitzitten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remain for the duration of; to sit for the duration of, to remain seated for the duration of</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to serve time (of a prison sentence) until completion</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the sense “to serve time until completion”, the term means that one <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not received a <a href = vnd.unilang:pardon.html>pardon</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> escaped and <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> at large.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:overgankelijk.html>overgankelijk</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:relatief.html>relatief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lange.html>lange</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoort.html>hoort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inderdaad.html>inderdaad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a>

***ultimatum.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimatum.html>ultimatum</a> (18330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:ultimatum.html>ultimatum</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ultimatus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">late, last final</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ultimō</i>.

***underdog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:underdog.html>underdog</a> (17279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">under-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dog</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underdog.html>underdog</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underdogs.html>underdogs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A competitor thought unlikely to win.
<ul><li><b>2004:</b> <i>The New Yorker,</i> 30 August 2004, p.40
<dl><dd>In Athens, the Americans are <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underdogs.html>underdogs</a></b> to the Chinese and the Canadians <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the Canadians!</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2014</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Steinberg, "<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/football/2014/mar/09/manchester-city-wigan-athletic-fa-cup">Wigan shock Manchester City in FA Cup again to reach semi-finals</a>", <i>The Guardian</i>, 9 March 2014:
<dl><dd>The visit of a Championship side would not normally send a shiver down their spine but they <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> that Wigan <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underdogs.html>underdogs</a></b> who would <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a> at their <a href = vnd.unilang:heels.html>heels</a> and that they possessed a potent bite if they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> not kept on a firm leash.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">little guy</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Somebody at a disadvantage.</li>
<li>A high swing wherein the person pushing the swing <a href = vnd.unilang:runs.html>runs</a> beneath the swing while the person being <a href = vnd.unilang:pushed.html>pushed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> at the forward limit of the arc.</li></ol>

***underlay.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a> (19514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">underleyen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">underleċġan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a>, prop, support</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">under-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lay</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">onderleggen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lay or put under</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unterlegen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">underlägga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">simple past tense of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">underlie</i></span></span></li></ol>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">underlays</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">underlaying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">underlaid</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To lay (something) underneath something else; to put under.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To provide a support for something; to raise or support by something laid under.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></b> a cut, plate, or the like, for printing</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To put a tap on (a shoe).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive, intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a vein, fault, or lode</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To incline from the vertical.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hade</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">underlei</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">under-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lay</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">underlays</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A layer (of earth, etc.) that lies under another; substratum.</li>
<li>A soft floor covering that lies under a carpet.</li>
<li>Anything that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> underlaid.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of paper pasted under woodcuts, stereotype plates, etc. in a form, to bring them up to the necessary level for printing.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>Lyrics</a>; or more specifically, the way in which <a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a> are assigned to musical notes.
<dl><dd><i>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underlay.html>underlay</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a> 3 <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear in <a href = vnd.unilang:handel.html>Handel</a>'s manuscript.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***unter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> (98191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">under</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">untar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*under</i> (compare Old Saxon <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">undar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hunsrik" class="extiw" title="w:Hunsrik">Hunsrik</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hrx">unne</i>, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i>, English <i>under</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>under</li>
<li>below</li>
<li>among, between
<ul><li><b>1919</b>, Walther <a href = vnd.unilang:kabel.html>Kabel</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/de:Irrende_Seelen" class="extiw" title="s:de:Irrende Seelen">Irrende Seelen</a></i>, Werner Dietsch Verlag, page 108:
<dl><dd>Unsere Unterredung wurde <a href = vnd.unilang:jetzt.html>jetzt</a> im leichten Plauderton geführt <a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a> ein harmloses Gespräch <b><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:guten.html>guten</a> Bekannten.
<dl><dd>Our discussion <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> now <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> in a light conversational tone like a harmless chat between friendly acquaintances.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> with; along with; accompanied by an action (often concessive)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> englische Sprache überlebte <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> normannische Eroberung <b><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></b> weitgehendem Verlust ihrer ursprünglichen Struktur.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The English language survived the <a href = vnd.unilang:norman.html>Norman</a> conquest, largely losing, however, its original structure.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> or regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> during</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The preposition <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used with accusative case if the verb indicates movement from one place to another, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used with dative case if the verb indicates location.</li>
<li>The sense “during” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> chiefly restricted to a few expressions, such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Woche</i> (“during the week, on weekdays”), in standard usage. In southern German speech it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used more freely.</li>
<li>With a definite article, the following contractions may occur: <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unterm</i> (= <a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> <span class="Latn" lang="de">dem</span>), <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">untern</i> (= <a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> <span class="Latn" lang="de">den</span>), and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unters</i> (= <a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>das</a></span>). These are non-obligatory contractions.</li></ul>
</body>

***up.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> up (65)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>up</b>
